<P>jay1atu bAsudeba kamaLA biLAsa

<P>to nAma sumarante baikuNThe bAsa | 1 |

<P>sehi pAdapadme nityeheM zaraNa

<P>zUdramuni sAroLa dAsa sebe se debI caraNa | 2 |

<P>baibasuta manu agastiMki kale pucchA

<P>pANDabe kaurobe kemante hoile ye kakSA | 3 |

<P>yujheSThi banabase rahile kemante

<P>y1ethira prastAba muni kahibAka mote | 4 |

<P>zuNa Aho baibasuta bidanti agasti

<P>pANDabongka banabAsa helA yeuM mati | 5 |

<P>aneka sAnande ye dharmara nandana

<P>zutra rohiNI yoge kaleka parasthAna | 6 |

<P>tuLamAsa kruSNapakSa puNa budhabAra

<P>amruta yoga rohiNI bruSa aTai se dinara | 7 |

<P>bALaba nAme karaNa byatipAta nAme yoga

<P>pan~chamI tithi sedina pANDabe pazile banamArga | 8 |
[MBO-04(1)-2]

<P>prathama dine rahile indra ye prazaste

<P>dhazAsana goDAi acchi karNNa zakuni sahite | 9 |

<P>dhana ratnamAna na puNa nianti se bane

<P>samasta chaDAi gheni boli AgyAM dilA driyodhana | 10 |

<P>indraprazastuM bAhAra hoile bahana

<P>Au dine bAruNAbante karanti gamana | 11 |

<P>yujheSThi bhIma arjuna nakuLa sahadeba

<P>kointA dropatI, subhadrAkaiM gheniNa caLanti pan~chu ye pANDaba | 12 |

<P>suranadIra tIre caLanti pan~chu bIre

<P>aMgeNa thilA tAMkara yeteka aLaMkAramAna

<P>samasta zodhiNa ye ghenilA dhuzAsana | 14 |

<P>bhImasenara zarIra kampai ati rAge

<P>dhuzAsanakaiM prahAra ki kariba sASTAMge | 15 |

<P>bAbu driyodhana boli kari yeuMNa mora bhrAta

<P>temanta sodara Ambhanta janme janme hou prApata | 17 |

<P>aLaMkAramAna yebe Ambhara tahiM thAnA

<P>banastare abazya ye pramAda Ambhnta paDanA | 18 |

<P>bAbu bipada kALakaiM dhana sundara bhAriyA

<P>paNDita jane y1ehAkaiM karanti paritejyA | 19 |

<P>ApaNe prahAraji kariba animite | 22 |
[MBO-04(1)-3]

<H>{@duryyodhanara apamAna@}

<P>zakuni boilA deba zuNimA kurupati

<P>pANDabe ye banabAsa gale pan~chukSatrI | 1 |

<P>keuNa sampade achanti paNDa putre

<P>kirAta rUpa dhari se buluchanti banaste | 2 |

<P>samadaNDa gheni saja hebA kurusAiM

<P>pANDabanta yibA Ambha sampada dekhAi | 3 |

<P>zakuni bacane AgyAM dilA driyodhana

<P>sAja ho samadaNDa mora sanya baLamAna

<P>maNDa ho aneka ratna bahuta ratha sanya | 4 |

<P>sAjanti rahubara aneka bIra tUra

<P>netara pAtAGga uDai ye phara hara | 5 |

<P>hIrA maNi mANikya ye birAjanti rathe

<P>ray1eNI prabhAte yehne dinakara nAthe | 6 |

<P>bahuta baLa can~chaLa ye asaMcepa hay1e

<P>kSepanti AkAze ye zeNApachIra prAy1e | 7 |

<P>yoddhAMkara zire ratna maNi ye mukuTa
